| <span data-ttu-id="ae5bf-707">Eingabe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ae5bf-707">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ae5bf-708">Wert</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ae5bf-708">Value</span></span> |
